The nose behind this fragrance is Olivier Pescheux. Top notes are Mandarin Orange, Madagascar Pepper, Lemon, Chinotto and Rosemary; middle notes are Geranium, Rose and Pepperwood™; base notes are Vanilla, Tonka Bean, Sandalwood, Texas Cedar, Patchouli and Oakmoss. </p><div v-pre class='fragrantica-blockquote'><p>Versace Eros Flame, is a flanker to the original masculine Eros from 2012. While the pillar is an aromatic-fougère, the new scent goes into a totally different direction with citrusy, spicy, woody, and ambery accords, described as "cold and hot, sweet and spicy, light and shadow."</p>

<p>The concept is based on an interpretation of passionate love, marketed as a fragrance for a "strong, passionate, self-confident man who is deeply in touch with his emotions."</p>

<p>Olivier Pescheux developed the composition as one of contrasts; the head notes are made to be vivacious and fresh with italian citruses, black pepper and rosemary. Pepperwood, geranium and rose facets are in the heart, before a warm base of woods, blended with tonka and vanilla.</p>

<p>The advertising campaign is a modern interpretation of Canova's iconic "Eros and Psyche" sculpture, where a man embraces a woman played by Gigi Hadid and Salomon Diaz. The campaign is shot by Steven Meisel.</p>

<p>Versace Eros Flame is available as a 30, 50, 100 and 200 ml Eau de Parfum, a 100 ml After Shave Lotion, a 100 ml After Shave Balm, a 75 ml Deodorant Stick, a 100 ml Deodorant and a 250 ml Shower Gel.</p></div><p class="reviewstrigger" style="font-size: smaller; color: #83a6c4">Read about this perfume in other languages: <a href="https://www.fragrantica.de/Parfum/Versace/Eros-Flame-52180.html" padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2220441">aaandrewwww</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-22"></span><fromunixtime unixtime="1729600872" class="vote-button-legend"></fromunixtime></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Just got a 30ML one for a great price ! Tested it out and here are some honest review. (personal thoughts only)<br />
<br />
Scent - (8/10)<br />
Although with a pretty harsh opening like medicine (maybe it's because of my first few times spraying), it dries down to a strong sweet vanilla + a bit spicy woody feel - sweet but spicy, formal and kinda playful at the same time. <br />
Also amazingly blended !!! Might be better than original !!!<br />
<br />
Longevity - (10/10)<br />
Crazy ahh longevity for sure :D On skin I get around 8hours (Sunny day), can't wait to try it on shirt, might get 12+ hours or 1 day &lt;3<br />
<br />
Projection (8/10)<br />
DO NOT OVERSPRAY !!!!! Do at most 2 sprays indoor :D I sprayed only once today and my desk-mate already be suffocating from my vanilla nuke :))))))<br />
<br />
Overall I don't really think you should blind buy if you judge this fragrance based on only trying original eros, they  low-key have some obvious differences. <br />
But even if you blind bought it, the scent is still acceptable and enjoying to wear !</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="52180"comment_id="2323616"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-Flame-52180.html?ccid=2323616#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2322546" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1986230">maxventuri</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-13">10/13/24 21:00</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This is a unique take on the original Eros DNA. Imagine the original sweet Eros scent, but replace the mint in the opening with a realistic chinotto note. It might not be as mass-pleasing as the original Eros but much more versatile thanks to the fresher opening. Though I still think it's a "party boy" fragrance just like the original Eros. It's not exactly what I would call "beast mode" but that doesn't mean it doesn't perform. In fact, it performs quite well on my skin. Value for money is good, especially if you can get it at a discounter (I got this fragrance with a tester box for only 50$). Overall it's a good fragrance targeted for the younger crowd who wants a more versatile/unique take on Versace Eros.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="52180"comment_id="2314997"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-Flame-52180.html?ccid=2314997#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2314390" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2180901">Cay Sid Orphia</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-07">10/07/24 11:09</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This is a great one that works well during Fall and Winter but honestly I could use it in Spring too and maybe cooler Summer nights. It's a smoother Eros with an opening that gives off a slightly spicy orange creamsicle vibe with plenty of bright personality. After the opening dries down the scent becomes a nice creamy peppermint or candy cane thanks to the sweetness of the vanilla and I'm guessing the spice of the Pepperwood. I'm surprised not many people have mentioned getting that peppermint vibe. Definitely an easy reach for cooler months of the year and really nice and smooth. The projection is above average for me and it lasts all day. I've heard some people say that you can't distinguish this between the original Eros after dry down. To me it has that similar Eros DNA but it is distinctly its own thing, so unless it was reformulated, that doesn't feel accurate. Definitely a welcomed fragrance in your collection so pick it up!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="52180"comment_id="2307890"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-Flame-52180.html?ccid=2307890#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2304178" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; It starts citrus, fresh and spicy and in the drydown it emerges intoa warm, sweet scent. The longevity is around 8-9 hours on my skin, great projection for the first 3-4 hours, after which it becomes less noticeable but still not a skin scent (this is based on 3 sprays). For the price i think this is a great quality fragrance and pretty safe choice since almost everybody likes it. Only downside for me is that it might be a little overwhelming if worn in office environment. In this case i would go with 1-2 sprays and probably spray an hour before i leave the house so it has some time to calm down. This being said i think it is versatile fragrance, pretty safe choice for blind buy and we could say compliment getter if that’s what you are aiming for. Warning: you can get nose blind to it, but don’t be fooled, people around you can still sense it.<br />
Layer with vetiver if you want more depth and mature scent.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="52180"comment_id="2286628"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-Flame-52180.html?ccid=2286628#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2286399" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Starts with a nice bittersweet citrus and spicy, after 20-30min it mellows out to a rosy vanilla scent. 10/10 Performance, I usually use about 2-3 sprays of this one, I would probably go for 1 in a close-quarter work environment and 2 absolute maximum in a large office with more personal space. Anymore than that you'll have to experiment based on your skin. Definitely don't start at more than 3 unless you're going to a club or somewhere outside and not shoulder-to-shoulder with others. Moderate to strong from 1-6 hours, moderate from 6-8th hour, 8-12th hour is pretty intimate to skin-level but I can usually still inhale and notice it on myself. Of course all skins and climates are different. 6/10 Smell. I love the scent overall but on my skin in particular, the vanilla is pretty strong without as much floral or spice as I would like and it really makes it smell like a creamy-sweet unisex fragrance. For me it smells like one of those Vanilla Bean Frappuccinos from Starbucks with a little bit of holiday spice. I've gotten compliments from ladies but also been told "You kind of smell like a girl" by some as well, which wasn't necessarily said like it was a bad thing but it's something to consider if that type of thing is a concern for you. We'll see if anything changes now that the weather is going to start cooling off more significantly. Definitely a winter/fall scent for me. Probably would be great for holiday gatherings, date nights when its chilly out, or if you just want something sweet on in the house while you be a winter homebody. I wouldn't call it "sexy" on me so much as romantic or comforting.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="52180"comment_id="2284847"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-Flame-52180.html?ccid=2284847#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2282940" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.86);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:2,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; If you have the original Eros I don't think you need this as I actually enjoy the original more.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="52180"comment_id="2272730"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-Flame-52180.html?ccid=2272730#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2270534" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2270534" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="local7"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1547197"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1547197.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="local7" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2270534ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck4x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2270534" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.84); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1547197">local7</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-03">09/03/24 15:52</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This frag punches so far above it's weight it's not even funny. This is far and away the best of the Eros line and stands apart. There is so much good to be said about it. It definitely does not get the credit it deserves. Versace has done such a good job with Eros in general in creating a pleasing fragrance that lasts. Flame replaces all the arguably "youthful" elements with beautiful and classy ones that free it of age classification. If anything it's far more mature. The citrus, spice and pepper are wonderful. It projects perfectly. It lasts a long time. It smells EXTREMELY good. It is so well balanced that it really starts to push into almost niche territory. This is such a beautiful and well done fragrance.<br />
<br />
I knew it was good by the way I discovered it. I was randomly testing a bunch of frags at Sephora a few weeks ago. Sometimes I get ahead of myself and am smelling one strip while already mentally trained on the next thing on the shelf. I try everything at random, cheap or expensive it doesn't matter. At one point I had made my way over to the Tom Fords and suddenly my brain interrupted my main train of thought looking at Oud Minérale with "HEY ... what you are now smelling is REALLY GOOD."<br />
<br />
I had forgotten that I even had a tester strip under my nose. I stopped myself in agreement, thinking "Dang, this IS good!" And then I realized I didn't even know what I was smelling. After rewinding my short term memory a minute or so I recalled the last thing I had sprayed -- Eros Flame. EROS? WAT!? And that is what startled me -- I never expected a reaction like that FROM EROS ANYTHING. Not even knowing what it was, I knew I had just experienced a completely unbiased reaction. And I don't normally have these kinds of reactions. That is what lead my to buy a bottle.<br />
<br />
I have had Eros EDP for over a year now. And it is solid for what it is. However while being a very pleasing fragrance it comes off as a little too youthful for me. Flame has everything good about the EDP but with all the right things dialed back (candied sweetness), and the right things added (black pepper, rosemary, blood orange) making it more mature and interesting, and with virtually the same powerful projection and longevity.<br />
<br />
While I'd rather not to talk about "value for your money," that really cannot be ignored here. Flame could easily be passed off as a PDM (the perfumer for this actually did create a PDM frag - Herod) or other niche and sell for three or four times the price. It is that well done. I have a lot of respect for Versace for creating a very good fragrance and keeping it reasonably priced. I almost don't want to do this review because I don't want to contribute to more people wearing this, but I'm doing it more to give credit where credit is due.<br />
<br />
If you are not really intro frags in general but want one REALLY GOOD fragrance which checks all the boxes, this should definitely be in your short list. You can wear this virtually any time, on any occasion and smell really nice.<br />
<br />
Good work Versace.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="52180"comment_id="2270534"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-Flame-52180.html?ccid=2270534#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2269039" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1385547">EMSFraghead</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-30">08/30/24 10:29</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>There's something about Eros Flame I just absolutely adore. I normally don't really like standard department store fragrances to be honest. I don't like super sweet fragrances either, and I initially thought I wouldn't like this because of that, but I was very wrong.<br />
<br />
 The standard Eros is something I like but wouldn't wear if that makes sense. The mint is very nice in both of these and is part of the reason I love flame. This has something more to it. <br />
<br />
 The mint and vanilla work together very well in this to kind of temper it from being cloying. There's a peppery, and citrusy smell that's almost cinnamon-esque. It's very comforting, and has this slight soapy hint that makes it nice. This has some sweetness to it that makes me not want to wear it in summer, but the added citrus and pepper make it a lot more wearable. It's got a green edge that I really like as well.<br />
<br />
 The only reason I don't wear this more is because it's Eros, I won't lie. I wear it around the house because I love it. I don't think anyone could really hate this, it's very pleasant. Everyone I know that has smelled this on me has really really liked it. I wear this more around Christmas because it's a very happy fragrance. <br />
<br />
 So overall, don't discount it just because it's a relative of a "clubbing" fragrance. It's very pleasant! This is one of those that when it gets discontinued people will really miss. There is a decent clone out there, I think it's Maison Alhambra, so if it does get discontinued we may still have a way to get some of the DNA.<br />
<br />
     Please don't spam this fragrance as a clubbing or seductive fragrance YouTube. It would be tragic if something so pleasant got turned into overspray hell. :(<br />
<br />
Just beautiful, makes me want to smell it all the time, and it's one I grab just to smell. If Eros didn't have the reputation it did I would wear this a ton and be really happy about it, call it peer pressure. <br />
<br />
 Give it a try! I think you'll like it! If this was a song it would be So Far Away by the Dire Straits.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="52180"comment_id="2265939"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-Flame-52180.html?ccid=2265939#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2263918" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; It is truly a universal compliment magnet. Any season, and place, and time, whatever. This gets it done. Just, go easy on the trigger. This is a performance monster, easy 10+hr for myself on my skin.<br />
<br />
Off of my skin, the uplifting, energetic, and lively citrus opening is an absolute showstopper. The citrus stays around past the opening, which lasts about 30-45min on my skin with room filling projection at 4 sprays, at which point it slowly transitions from an energetic burst of citrus; to a lively and bright, sparkly pepper forward mid with sweet vanilla/tonka undertones and light pops of citrus throughout. <br />
<br />
This whole portion lasts about 5hours with quite a nice scent bubble, just over arms length I'd like to say, obviously with certain notes fading and others becoming more prominent. <br />
<br />
After the mid, it dries down in such a surprising way where the chinotto and orange come back around and meld with the vanilla and tonka to provide a sweet, juicy citrus supported by the smooth sandalwood and cedar, and a touch of clean patchouli to give depth. This all provides one of the most well rounded experiences I have come across yet, my wife absolutely loves it at every stage throughout the day and night, and my coworkers give my compliments pretty regularly. 10/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2258217" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="CowberryEnjoyer"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2201245"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="CowberryEnjoyer" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2258217ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2258217" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.9); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2201245">CowberryEnjoyer</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-23">08/23/24 05:31</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I'm absolutely blown away by this.<br />
<br />
If you've ever smelled the melissa plant - a close relative of mint - you'll know exactly what the top notes are like. It smells *exactly* like a basket filled with lemon slices and fresh bundles of melissa. Extremely loud, fresh, exciting and uplifting *without* being obnoxious, harsh or synthetic. I'm extremely impressed with how crisp, clear, natural and defined the top notes are. You can almost *see* the lemon and melissa cocktail under your nose - what a beautiful blend.<br />
<br />
The opening is definitely my favorite part of the fragrance. The sillage at this point was also impressive with just 3 sprays.<br />
<br />
My least favorite part is the mid notes. But make no mistake, they're still really nice. The lemon and melissa become more subdued, making way for some mint, and a touch of masculine spiciness paired with a sweet vanilla.<br />
<br />
The base notes are to die for. A slightly spicy and masculine yet absolutely irresistible vanilla - gorgeous. I couldn't help but keep smelling myself.<br />
<br />
The performance was also insane: it lasted as a skin scent for nearly 24 hours - that included a few hours of being outdoors, several instances of lovemaking, and a good night's sleep.<br />
<br />
I also don't understand why some think this isn't a summer fragrance. For a summer day outdoors, this is perfect because of the invigorating citrus top notes, and the persistent fresh spiciness throughout the mid and base notes.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2255835" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="senpaiwavy"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1483800"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1483800.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="senpaiwavy" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Giorgio-Armani/Armani-Code-Eau-de-Parfum-65581.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.65581.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Armani Code Eau de Parfum"title="Armani Code Eau de Parfum"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2255835ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2255835" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.72); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1483800">senpaiwavy</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-20">08/20/24 23:41</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>The Eros Flame batch was made last year, but I bought it in late January this year, so it has been macerating for the past 7 months.<br />
<br />
The presentation isn’t bad. It's just a box, just like the other Eros in the same bottle. But I do like the design. It has a Greek pattern border. Other than that, and the Madusa logo, I wouldn’t say it’s generic; it’s minimalist with some Versace flair to it. The bottle is weighty, and the atomizer is good.<br />
<br />
I’ll test the smell by applying petroleum jelly to the back of my hand and then spray the cologne on the area. I won’t talk about projection because I think it’s arbitrary since you can aLWaYs OvErSpRaY (I overspray quite frequently. I only get compliments when I do. Continue Hating.)<br />
<br />
Immediate:<br />
<br />
It smells hella citrusy. I don’t remember being this strong in citrus. When I open the box, it just spews out citrus, but that probably came with age. After dry down, the vanilla comes into play. It smells as if Berry Blends only sold lemonade, orange juice, and Sara Lee Honey Wheat Bread but replaced the honey with vanilla and held the crust.<br />
<br />
1 Hour Later:<br />
<br />
Now, this is epic. The citrus toned down a lot but was still present, along with the vanilla. It starts to bring out more of the aromatic, rose, and slight pepper notes. Fragrantica says there’s Pepperwood(™) in the heart note. I’ve never heard nor smelled Pepperwood(™) alone before, but since it’s mentioned, it smells like what it sounds like. So far, it smells like HomeDepot had a FFAATT fruit and flower section.<br />
<br />
I would say this is technically a 4 season cologne, but I would only wear it between 30 to 65 degrees Fahrenheit (-1.1111 to 18.3333 degrees Celsius) weather with no precipitation and shy away from it if it’s windy<br />
<br />
Overall, I would get another bottle of this. This is my second bottle and I’m a third into it. I’ll give it an 8/10, an A tier cologne. It’s not as crazy as some of my other favorites, but it’s well above average.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="52180"comment_id="2255835"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-Flame-52180.html?ccid=2255835#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2255464" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2040463">Pick</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-27">07/27/24 02:30</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This was made to be an improvement on the Eros DNA, in that sense I think it does it's job, but I still find it makes the same mistakes that Eros makes.<br />
<br />
So first of all, the problem with Eros is that it wasn't very smooth, that was my main issue with Versace Eros, it was simply too easy to recognize all the notes you were getting. <br />
Think of Y edp, the average person couldn't tell you what the notes are by just smelling it but if you gave someone Eros they could easily tell you it's mainly apple and vanilla, now I believe Eros flame improved this, the orange goes well with the vanilla and its definitely more smooth than the original Eros, however it still has the same rough DNA that the original eros had, it still doesn't feel very well blended, but I do think the orange was an improvement.<br />
Now as for the scent, it kind of reminds you of orange vanilla ice-cream without the milkiness and without the refreshing sensation of ice-cream, it's very close to being a gourmand but it just barely misses it.<br />
Just don't be lazy and go to your local Sephora to smell it before buying it, many people will like it, many people won't.<br />
<br />
Keep in mind I am very biased because it's very close to the original Eros and, even though I hate it when people say a cologne is overdone, Eros was and still is the signature scent of so many people in my school and I just cannot get the scent of sweat and body oder mixed with the apple vanilla out of my head when smelling any eros</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; Because of the sweetness of this transition form, I feel like I'm eating tangerine/peach with chocolate...<br />
<br />
I can't say a single bad word about its longevity. A washed garment of mine smells on average for about 5 days. If this is a cotton sweater, it has a performance of over 7+ days. On the skin, it gives an intense performance of 8-12 hours depending on the weather conditions... padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2108424">Cosmos_PMF</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-19">07/19/24 13:52</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This is the most underrated modern release ever. The definition of "it grows on me so masterfully" type of scent.<br />
<br />
I remember testing it few months ago with my frisnd and we both agreed on it smelling like "masculine sweat" with strong projection. But I decided to give it another chance and get the full bottle.<br />
I was shocked on the first actual day wears.<br />
<br />
As a scent profile this has a similar versace Eros edp backbone but with many twists. <br />
Wearing this fragrance is one of the best journeys you can experience<br />
The sensation while smelling the opening for example is unbelievable, mandarin with fresh spices and when you take your nose off you feel that creamy vanilla undertone which makes it a very sexy blend. If I can describe it photorealistically, a citrus basket with melted vanilla around it, and then some soft pepper spices are added inside the oranges core.<br />
<br />
The performance is awesome, 7-9hrs with moderate to strong projection.<br />
<br />
When it comes to versatility, most people say it's cold weather only but I'll definitely disagree, it does have the reminiscent minty fresh aspect of the Eros edp, which makes it suitable for daily wear too. Spring, summer nights, fall/autumn, winter. Night outs, partying, even a creative daily signature<br />
<br />
The bottle is iconic of course, with nice glass texture, the atomizer is average, the cap is great too. <br />
<br />
This is in my top 5 fav colognes from my collection, or even of all time. <br />
<br />
Versace Eros Flame: creative, underrated, very sexy blend of freshness spiceness and creamy vanilla, absolutely amazing release, although not very mass appealing. Lights up your mood while wearing it, while keeping a mysterious vibe. 9.5/10. Just wow</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="52180"comment_id="2223571"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-Flame-52180.html?ccid=2223571#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2223057" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.85);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I have tested the OG before and it is good but not as interesting as this flanker. <br />
<br />
This is 🔥🔥🔥 an awesome release. Not for older gentleman but still good for 40 and downwards. <br />
<br />
The opening is very citrus heavy with the rosemary in the frontline lifting the lemon and orange high in the sky. <br />
<br />
It then smells green and aromatic fresh if that makes sense. <br />
<br />
But, after the first hour, this fragrance begins to shine ✨ as bright as a diamond with flames in the background. <br />
<br />
It becomes a vanilla orange peppery smooth rose like powder smell which is so intoxicating. The rosemary is still there but now at the back supporting the vanilla mixed with just enough orange and pepper. <br />
<br />
Lovely, like this so-far and I give it a 9 out of 10 for the scent. <br />
<br />
Will give more feedback with regard's to experience with people and weather.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="52180"comment_id="2217476"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-Flame-52180.html?ccid=2217476#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2217302" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I see it mainly as a vanilla fragrance, a very decent well structured one.<br />
<br />
The opening is deceiving I thought mmm it citrusy warm suits winter more but after the opening I said this more fun to be worn in summer because after the first 20 to 30 minutes its more smooth, light and cooling... the powdery aspect is amazing I have no idea which component adds it but it's what makes it smooth and soft like an AC in hot weather...<br />
<br />
It's long lasting 8+ H, projects well , smells amazing on clothes and the transition is slower on fabric so you'll get more warmth and spice  but on skin its very smooth airy and gentle.<br />
<br />
I always believed that Versace fragrances are very mass appealing and this one is no exception... it needs multiple testing to be appreciated properly.<br />
<br />
I love it,  8.5/10 in general... 10/10 as a vanilla fragrance because its more masculine and versatile than many men vanilla fragrances in the market.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; But honestly I have 2 that I constantly go back to and this is one of them! I have yet to find a summer fragrance that performs as well as this, smells ass good, and lasts as long. It is a perfect blend of Citrus and tonka notes that is sure to be a complement getter and you will not need to worry about refreshing everyday at lunch like damn near every fragrance  out there even at $300+ price points! That's why the YouTubers and the influencers and the "Frasier &amp; Niles Crane" of the fragrance world hate it! It's not a billion dollars/ounce and this ISH is fire!!  Never wore it during the winter and never wore the EDT version or the OG Eros, so I can't speak on those. But this is Eros Flame EDP is a solid fragrance.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="52180"comment_id="2186825"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-Flame-52180.html?ccid=2186825#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2186674" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:4,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1057186">Sq_One</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-11">06/11/24 17:07</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I started getting into fragrances earlier this year and this was the first purchase since. Not only a completely blind buy (I've never smelled Eros previously) but an also brave one as I bought a 100mL bottle on eBay for $35. After watching videos regarding presentation and such, I confirmed that it was in fact real but the smell of it pretty much confirmed that for me already. It opens with a very sharp citrus, almost likened to a citrus cleaner or furniture polish the more I smell it, with a bit of spice and warmth behind it. Yes, it does have a synthetic citrus smell but everything else kind of evens it out enough for it to still be an enjoyable fragrance. While the warmth and spice of it leans more towards cooler weather, the citrus does come through enough to make it more versatile for warmer weather if not oversprayed. This is very much a parfum in that aspect. It easily lasts for 6 hours and projects well within 6 feet for the first hour or two. A very beautiful, well put together fragrance that's sure to grab attention.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="52180"comment_id="2185341"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-Flame-52180.html?ccid=2185341#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2185235" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I was expecting something to the original Eros, which I have and love, but it goes its own direction. This is just wonderful in every way possible, the citrus and chinotto in the opening is so good. <br />
<br />
In the mid I can begin to pick more similarities to the original Eros, but it’s still unique carrying the orange citrus and rose smell through to the dry down. Dry down is super smooth and creamy vanilla that reminds me of the creamy smoothness in blue de Chanel EDP. <br />
<br />
As far as occasions go this works anytime in winter, fall, and spring. For summer I’d recommend using it at evening/night as in high heat it can be too much. Something I can’t wait to do is wear this to an evening barbecue with family, it would do fenomenal in those kind of situations.<br />
<br />
This fragrance really impressed me. 10/10 for me guys, the entire Eros line is good but hands down flame is my new favorite.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="52180"comment_id="2173175"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-Flame-52180.html?ccid=2173175#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2172705" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Performance: 9/10<br />
Longevity: 10/10<br />
Sillage: 5/10<br />
Price: 9/10<br />

In the opening there’s an over powering orange note that I don’t love. But as it dries down there’s more vanilla and pepper but the citrus is still pretty prominent. The performance is insane, 8 hours with super strong projection and nice silage. I’m ready to try out Eros energy when it releases</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="52180"comment_id="2160397"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-Flame-52180.html?ccid=2160397#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2159681" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; This is a gorgeous counterpart to the mainline Eros. Both are super versatile with amazing performance but I'd say this leans to warmer seasons while Eros leans to colder seasons, but both can be worn all year round. This is a fresh, citrusy, peppery twist with the classic cedar, geranium and vanilla core from Eros. The chinotto and orange are delicious while the pepper and rosemary add something different and stick with the fragrance all the way. Definitely for younger guys and slightly less common than Eros.<br />
<br />
Top notes: Orange, chinotto, rosemary, pepper<br />
Middle notes: Geranium, pepper<br />
Base notes: Vanilla, woods (mainly cedar), pepper<br />
<br />
Longevity: 4/5<br />
Sillage: 4/5<br />
Scent: 5/5<br />
Design: 5/5<br />
Gender: Masculine<br />
Overall: 5/5</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="52180"comment_id="2145570"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-Flame-52180.html?ccid=2145570#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2145495" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/272328">Neyzen</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2021-08-28">08/28/21 15:02</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I can't understand why this fragrance is so underrated..<br />
<br />
Is it generic and mainstream? Yes! So what?<br />
<br />
"Let's bash this mainstream flanker and everyone will think that we are fragrance experts..."<br />
<br />
I hate the fragrance nerds on fragratica. If a designer fragrance is extremely succesful (like 1 million, Eros, code profumo, etc), they automatically hate that fragrance. Actually, what they hate is its popularity, marketing, or the simple fact that such a cheapy is far better than most of their niche collections. And they automatically criticize each and every flanker to be released.<br />
<br />
They hate gems like this one, and praise some stinking niche fragrance or an expensive designer hyped among the fragrance community, because it is "creative and original". Yet if you believe these "experts" and buy one of their recommendations, ordinary people around you will consider that you smell "peculiar" at best. At worst, some will consider that you are stinking!<br />
<br />
This is a mainstream, mass pleaser designer fragrance, aimed at extending the success of original Eros to a wider audience (the reason of all the hate). But there is nothing wrong about it. Most people will think that you smell amazing. Ladies will consider that you smell sexy, and some of them will compliment you fanatically.<br />
<br />
Its longevity and projection is above the roof, so your money is not spent for some scented water with less projection than your shampoo. And you don't pay a fortune for a niche to smell like the purse of an old lady.<br />
<br />
I wear this during summer and Eros EDT/EDP in winter. Personally, I like this more than original Eros, since I don't like original's minty opening. And I've been complimented wearing this more than the original. People even stopped me to ask the name of my fragrance on various occasions, maybe because few recognize Eros Flame.<br />
<br />
No one at the office considered that it is offensive. And my office mate (who is a female) bought Eros Flame for her husband after asking me. I consider that it is much more versatile than the original Eros and it can be worn during any occasion or season.<br />
<br />
Please do not underestimate any member of the Eros line. Each of them smell amazing and each is a girl magnet. Buy whichever pleases you, and you will not be dissapointed. Period.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="52180"comment_id="1400364"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-Flame-52180.html?ccid=1400364#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1142834" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1142834" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="007peter"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1079008"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1079008.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="007peter" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1142834ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck8x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1142834" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.78); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1079008">007peter</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2020-02-07">02/07/20 18:05</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>**********************************************<br />
I ♥ original EROS, but I ♥♥♥ Flame more<br />
**********************************************<br />
I ♥ the original EROS, my reviews has one of the most balloons awards (yet) I now prefer Flame, here is why: <br />
<br />
1. <b>Better Blended (more smooth)</b>.  Original Eros start with a Fresh Lemon &amp; Fresh Mint opening, then do a sudden left-turn toward a Seductive Sweet Vanilla drydown.  This Dr. Jekyll &amp; Mr. Hyde personality grabs attention (but) can also came off rather Jarring, non-smooth, Immature, and not-well blended.  This is where FLAME wins for me.  It is a better (blended) fragrances from the beginning to the end.  The sweet Mandarin Orange blended well with a sweet Vanilla drydown.  There are no sudden Left Turn, no sudden change-of-character, no sudden switch-of-character.   <br />
<br />
<br />
2. <b>More Mature, Less Attention Grabbing</b>.  Flame, due to its smooth blended nature, doesn't grab attention like the original EROS.  It is the more Mature Brother to Eros, the type of men who is Self-Confident without the need to call attention to oneself.  A good analogy are:<br />
<br />
Original Eros = Rapper <b>Vanilla Ice</b> from 1990.  Loud, Crude, in-your-face, attention grabber.  I'm Proud, I'm Loud, don't ignore me.<br />
<br />
Eros Flame = Actor <b>Ryan Gosling</b>.  Classically Handsome but never shout, never call for attention, never try to stand out, dress conservatively.  It is knowing who you are as a MAN without the need to shout.   <br />
<br />
3. Orange-Peel Vanilla is Seductive....  Less clubbing but more DATE NIGHT appropriate<br />
<br />
***********************************************<br />
Flame is stronger &gt; (Reformulated) EROS<br />
***********************************************<br />
Flame Haters seem to have forgotten that EROS has sadly been reformulated.  EROS is no longer the 10hrs powerhouse from 2016, but a reduced average 5~6 hrs longevity.   I agree with User (Jerry Dee) from post below that: "FLAME lasts better than the reformulated Eros"<br />
<br />
• 10 hrs+ Original 2016 Eros, sometimes next day<br />
• 5~6 hrs 2019 Eros from Macy<br />
• 6~7 hrs 2019 Eros Flame from Macy<br />
<br />
**********************************************************************<br />
Flame better with AGE (35+), EROS better with teen~college<br />
**********************************************************************<br />
Ultimately AGE play a huge factor here.  If you're a 20s something needing a Clubbing Fragrance for attention, by all means buy the Reformulated EROS for attention.  On the other hand, if you're a 35+ professional, who don't go to clubs anymore, than the new FLAME with its "Mature Subtle Seductive" Charm is  the better fit.  <br />
<br />
• EROS is the better Clubbing fragrance for 20 something<br />
• FLAME is the better DATE NIGHT fragrance for 35+.  <br />
<br />
No hate, just TRUTH.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="52180"comment_id="1142834"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-Flame-52180.html?ccid=1142834#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1166422" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/33823">ghent32</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2019-02-20">02/20/19 18:49</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Ok, so this one caught me by surprise because I really didn’t think there was much of any other direction to take Eros.<br />
<br />
Flame is very pleasantly surprising. The top notes, for me, are stunningly good. I keep hearing people call this synthetic or generic? Yea, I don’t see that at all. I think many folks are not familiar with the note of chinotto, but this chinotto not to my nose is quite realistic. <br />
<br />
This opens with a massive fresh/slightly green buckets of oranges mixed with a very silky smooth vanilla, very mass appealing. Toward the dry down it goes more toward tonka &amp; Vanilla with a slight orange hovering &amp; a touch of spice.<br />
<br />
This is sweet, but not overly sweet or gourmand. I personally don’t think this one resembles Eros much at all, really it’s own fragrance.<br />
<br />
Longevity is outstanding, easily 10+ hours on skin &amp; 16+ on clothing.<br />
<br />
Silage is good - projection is just moderate for me, but pretty good. <br />
<br />
Eros Flame is definitely more smooth &amp; well blended as Eros came off sharp at times to me.<br />
<br />
I give Eros Flame an 8.5/10.<br />
<br />
Versace is very consistent with good releases.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="52180"comment_id="1033650"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-Flame-52180.html?ccid=1033650#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div>                            <reviews-infinity :random-colors="[&quot;#fefcee&quot;,&quot;#faf7ec&quot;,&quot;#f9f9f3&quot;,&quot;#f8f9ec&quot;,&quot;#fffdea&quot;,&quot;#faf9fb&quot;,&quot;#faf5f2&quot;,&quot;#f7f4f2&quot;]" :perfume-id="52180" sentiment="positive"></reviews-infinity>

padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/659619">Raidthesaladbar</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2018-11-03">11/03/18 09:30</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Ran into a bottle of this by chance today, and it was exactly what I expected: Very pleasant, generic, and completely uninteresting - I think the popular euphemism for this kind of thing is a "crowd-pleaser".<br />
<br />
There were quite a few people who thought this would somehow be a novel or creative fragrance (probably based on the accords it's supposedly built of) - but don't be taken in by marketing BS.<br />
<br />
I have no idea what chinotto smells like <i>au naturel</i>, but here in Italy it is widely used for digestifs and soft drinks, imbuing them with a bitter-citric flavour. If that sounds off-putting to you, don't worry - Eros Flame smells absolutely nothing like chinotto. It has a generic fruity top, like someone layered several BOSS colognes. All that sits on the familiar, vaguely nutty base that the large brands have been trying to convince us is "tonka" ever since actual coumarin went out of fashion. Window-dress with the usual suspects (barely noticeable spices, woody-ambery backdrop, vanilla base), et voilà - déjà-vu in a bottle. That'd be 98€, please.<br />
<br />
Edit: Ouff, I just noticed the far drydown on the back of my hand, a hollow woody amber with a side of synthetic-smelling rosemary. Forget what I said about this thing being "pleasant".</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="52180"comment_id="997232"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-Flame-52180.html?ccid=997232#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1042183" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%;
